***серый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рый</a> (528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*śěrъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">séryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сере́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:сереть.html>сере́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>grey, gray
<dl><dd></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dull, dreary</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unremarkable, mundane, mediocre</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dim, ignorant, uneducated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> not quite legal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>получа́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рую</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарплата.html>зарпла́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">polučátʹ <b>séruju</b> zarplátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get paid <b>under the table</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">séryj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рого</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рых</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wolf</li>

***сестра.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестра́</a> (833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sestra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swésōr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sestrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестры́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сёстры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестёр</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sister
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">сво́дная <a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svódnaja sestrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stepsister</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvojúrodnaja <b>sestrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cousin, first cousin</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trojúrodnaja <b>sestrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">second cousin</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родной.html>родна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rodnája <b>sestrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sister (sibling)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медицинский.html>медици́нская</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">medicínskaja <b>sestrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">nurse</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сесть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a> (288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сѣсти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sěsti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sěsti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sestʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sit down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сел</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:диван.html>дива́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ря́дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>дру́гом</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>sel</b> na diván rjádom s moím drúgom.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>sat</b> on the couch next to my friend.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>се́ла</a></b> бли́же <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:настольный.html>насто́льной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпе</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>séla</b> blíže k nastólʹnoj lámpe.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>sat</b> near the tabletop lamp.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be imprisoned</li>
<li><i>(of an electrical battery or accumulator)</i> to become flat, to die</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">setʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сетевой.html>сетево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">setevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> network
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сетевой.html>сетево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:протокол.html>протоко́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>setevój</b> protokól</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>network</b> protocol</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> electrotechnology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> power, mains
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сетевой.html>сетево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шнур.html>шнур</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>setevój</b> šnur</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>power</b> cable/cord</span></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">setʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">net</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>net, netting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проволочный.html>про́волочная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">próvoločnaja <b>sétka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">wire <b>netting</b>; wire mesh</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">моски́тная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">moskítnaja <b>sétka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mosquito <b>net</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mesh, gauze</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> net
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjač zadél <b>sétku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the ball touched the <b>net</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:касание.html>каса́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kasánije <b>sétki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">contact with the <b>net</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отправить.html>отпра́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otprávitʹ mjač v <b>sétku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>net</b> the ball</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>string bag</li>
<li>luggage rack <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a train</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>grid, graticule</li>
<li>scale
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:налоговый.html>нало́говая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nalógovaja <b>sétka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">tax rate schedule</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>reticulum, bonnet, the second compartment of the stomach of a ruminant</li></ol>

***сеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сеть</a> (1747)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sětь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">net, snare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">syć</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sieć</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">síť</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">сѣть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sětĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">seś</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">setʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>се́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>се́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сете́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>net (used for catching fish), mesh</li>
<li>grid</li>
<li>network, system</li></ol>

***сечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечь</a> (10417)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sěťi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sek-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́сечь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut (up), to chop, to hew, to slash to pieces; to cleave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повинный.html>пови́нную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:меч.html>меч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечёт</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">povínnuju gólovu i meč ne sečót</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a fault confessed is half redressed</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">even a sword doesn't <b>cut</b> the head of the one who confesses</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to catch, to latch on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечёшь</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sečóšʹ</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">got it?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to know something <i>(about)</i>, to know the ropes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечёт</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on v étom déle ne <b>sečót</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he doesn't <b>know</b> a (damn) thing about this matter</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́сечь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flog, to whip, to lash <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to whip or scourge someone or something as punishment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">séjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеялка.html>се́ялка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">séjalka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеялка.html>се́ялки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеялка.html>се́ялки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеялка.html>се́ялок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>seeder, sowing machine</li></ol>

***сеять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a> (7801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sě̀jati</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sě̀ti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*seh₁-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">serō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">séjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посеять.html>посе́ять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose, to squander</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spread (an idea, fear etc.)</li></ol>

<li>concise, brief, succinct</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сжать.html>сжать</a> (3822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>to contract, to shrink</li>
<li>to be clenched
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зу́бы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сжаться.html>сожму́тся</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Moí zúby <b>sožmútsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My teeth will be <b>clenched</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сжаться.html>сожмётся</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mojá ruká <b>sožmjótsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My hand will be <b>clenched</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be compressed <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of gas or liquid</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>Два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:литр.html>ли́тра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сжаться.html>сжа́лись</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dva lítra vodý <b>sžálisʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Two liters of water <b>were compressed</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сжать.html>сжать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sžatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сжигаемый.html>сжига́емый</a></b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.  <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>  — <a href = vnd.unilang:сжечь.html>сожжённый</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-жиг-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-ем</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><i>страд. прич. <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. вр.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сжигать.html>сжига́ть</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>Лицо́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:морщиться.html>морщилось</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>черне́ло</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> обугливался, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:сжигаемый.html>сжига́емый</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:невидимый.html>неви́димым</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огнём</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%93%D0%BE%D1%80%D1%8C%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%B9,_%D0%9C%D0%B0%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BC" class="extiw" title="w:Горький, Максим">Максим <a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>Го́рький</a></a>, «<a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>Жизнь</a> Матвея Кожемякина», <span class="example-date">1910</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>г</a>.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span></li>
